

--- SOURCE: https://checkbook.ohio.gov ---

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

[ ![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Graphics/covid_btn.png)](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Coronavirus/)
The Ohio Checkbook serves as the singular and most trusted resource for Ohioans to obtain both local and state financial information. The Ohio Checkbook is a result of a joint initiative from two first-of-their-kind sites, Ohiocheckbook.com and Ohio's Interactive Budget. The collective effort enhances government transparency by providing real-time state financial and transactional data. Users can view online government spending, as well as how revenue is allocated.
_Note: Local Government salary data information is provided during the 1st quarter of the calendar year. While data is submitted voluntarily, some entities update information on a quarterly and/or monthly basis._
_Pension Checkbook data is updated annually._
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.
[![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/coronavirus.svg) See how much the State has   
received and spent on the Coronavirus](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Coronavirus/)

# Expenses By Type  - Capital+Funding
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/state-expenses-type.svg)
The Expense Types presentation shows spending for Ohio agencies grouped by the type of expense. Users can drill to agency and individual transactions.

Download Visual  Get Short URL  Questions about this Visual 
![](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/Gifs/large-loader-snake.gif%20) Sending Message - Please do not close this window
AN UNKNOWN ERROR HAS OCCURED
Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
**[DataOhio Portal](https://data.ohio.gov/wps/portal/gov/data/view/ohio-checkbook)** to download a comprehensive report of State data _(does not include local government and school districts data)._

# ALI Expense Breakdown  - School+Foundation+Funding
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/state-icon.svg)
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.
### Please select a fund:
- Select One -  Appropriation Line Item Group Load Visual
Performance Test: 
Marks Selection: 
URL Parameters: 
Download Visual  Get Short URL  Questions about this Visual 
![](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/Gifs/large-loader-snake.gif%20) Sending Message - Please do not close this window
AN UNKNOWN ERROR HAS OCCURED
Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
**[DataOhio Portal](https://data.ohio.gov/wps/portal/gov/data/view/ohio-checkbook)** to download a comprehensive report of State data _(does not include local government and school districts data)._

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

# Privacy Policy
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/privacy-icon.svg)
This policy describes how the Ohio Office of Budget and Management (OBM) and the Office of the Ohio Treasurer (TOS) collects, stores, and uses information about Ohioans, to be assessed against new technologies, business practices, and to meet our visitors changing needs.
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.
This Web site does not collect personally identifiable information (such as name, address, telephone number, etc.) unless you provide such information voluntarily through an online form or e-mail. Please be aware that, subject to certain legal exceptions, most documents and records maintained by the state of Ohio, including electronic data, are public records under Ohio law. Therefore, information submitted through this Web site may be subject to disclosure pursuant to a public records request and may be shared with other agencies as required by law.
Your personal information will never be sold or rented and will not be disclosed or shared with third parties not affiliated with the state of Ohio.
In order to generate usage statistics to help us improve our Web site, we automatically collect certain information on every visitor. This information does not disclose "personal identifiers" (such as name, address, telephone number, e-mail address, etc.) Each time a request is made to view a page within this site, our server creates a log file capturing generic user information such as type of Internet browser or computer operating system, date and time of visit and the IP (Internet Protocol) address of the individual computer (or proxy server) making the request, and the Internet address of the site from which you may have linked to this site.
All information collected by way of server log files is used in aggregate form only, and is analyzed for trends and statistics.
Temporary cookies may be created when necessary to complete a transaction, to process data submitted to us online or to facilitate ongoing interaction. They do not contain personally identifiable information. Information collect on our Web site, including cookies, may also be subject to disclosure because of a public records request.
We take very seriously the integrity of the information and systems that we maintain. Therefore, we have instituted security measures for all information systems under our control. These security measures are designed to identify attempts to tamper with this Web site. Information collected through these security measures may be used in connection with a criminal prosecution or other legal proceedings.
The State of Ohio has established procedures to ensure that every reasonable effort is made to address our customer's privacy concerns. If you have comments or concerns regarding our privacy policy, please visit our contact page to talk to a member of our staff.
**Ohio Office of Budget and Management**  
30 E. Broad Street, 34th Floor  
Columbus, OH 43215 
For questions or comments regarding the expenditure database or its usefulness ([ORC 113.74](https://codes.ohio.gov/ohio-revised-code/section-113.74)):   
[Questions@OhioCheckbook.gov](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Contact/)
**Ohio Treasurer**  
30 E. Broad Street, 9th Floor  
Columbus, OH 43215

Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.
# About the Ohio Checkbook
The Ohio Checkbook serves as the singular and most trusted resource for Ohioans to obtain local and state financial information. In November 2019, the Ohio Checkbook became a collective result of Lt. Governor Jon Husted and Ohio Treasure Robert Sprague unveiling a joint initiative aimed at enhancing government transparency by providing Ohioans real-time financial and transactional data.
The Ohio Checkbook is the result of this effort bringing together features from two first-of-their-kind - the Ohiocheckbook.com and Ohio’s Interactive Budget. Upon its launch in 2014, OhioCheckbook.com set a new national standard for transparency in government and was recognized three times by the U.S. Public Interest Research Group as being ranked number one in transparency for providing online access to government spending data. In six years, more than 1,150 local government entities around Ohio partnered with the Treasurer’s office to make financial data available through the website.
Ohio's Interactive Budget was launched in 2016, by the Ohio Office of Budget and Management (OBM), as a first of its kind comprehensive open checkbook that enabled users to see not only how state money is spent, but also how revenue is generated and allocated via the state budget. The Ohio Interactive Budget site was an extension of the state accounting system that provided the public access to the financial and transactional data maintained in the state's accounting system.
Each site's functionality and purpose has been preserved in the new Ohio Checkbook site, which merged the cutting-edge features of OhioCheckbook.com and Ohio’s Interactive Budget, placing them under one roof.
_If you have questions about Checkbook.Ohio.Gov, please email us by using the contact form_

# User's Guide
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/guide-icon.svg)
A quick guide explaining how The Ohio Checkbook operates when downloading data, navigating the menu, accessing information in detail, and changing views.
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.
#### Purpose
The Ohio Checkbook provides a searchable online database of both local and state real-time financial and transactional information. According to Section 126.21 of the Ohio Revised Code, the Ohio Checkbook retains transparency of the state accounting system through the site. 
Ohioans can utilize this information to view how both local and state collect, budget and spend public resources. Financial information is provided in multiple formats with the capability to drill in detail from summarized data to individual expense transactions. Citizens can use this information to make educated decisions and provide feedback to their legislators and other public servants who work for the State of Ohio.
#### The Home Page
Users can enter The Ohio Checkbook viewing real-time data filtering, while accessing state and local financial information, such as: Year-to-Year State Revenue, State Budget (by function), State Spending (by expense type), State Contracts, Year-to-Year State Spending and Employee Salaries. The FAQ page and Glossary are additional tools available for resource. 
#### Menu
The left-side menu is the primary source for navigating throughout The Ohio Checkbook site. The menu is permanently positioned on the left-side of each page as it contains links to all items on the home page, while offering a drop-down functionality to link to sub-pages within the site. 
#### "Real-Time" Data Filtering
Filtering the real-time data enables users to retrieve progressively more detailed financial information simply by clicking on the data fields, such as: bar graphs, pie charts and line graphs. When attempting to return to a previous view when filtering, users should use the left side of the visual to return to a previously viewed level. Clicking the browser's back button will return visitors to the Ohio Checkbook home page.
#### Guides
When filtering real-time data, a guide will appear on the left side of the screen to inform users where they are in the pathway. The guide allows users to jump to previous level of filtering without needing to start at the original drill path. 
#### Searches
The Ohio Checkbook contains a search bar located on the home page that allows users to type a word or phrase, the search engine will automatically populate with potential terms. Users may click on the term that best fits their search and will be directed to that page within the Ohio Checkbook site. 
#### Changing Views
When viewing data in the Ohio Checkbook site, users can choose the display of financial information in a different format opposed to the default. Majority of data is defaulted in bar graph or pie chart form., however users can toggle their view by clicking "Change View" on the page and select a new option from the drop-down menu. 
#### Downloads
Real-time data shown on the Ohio Checkbook is available for download in PDF and Excel format. In the upper right corner of each page, to download click the "Download" button and select a file type to download the data.
**Ohio Office of Budget and Management**  
30 E. Broad Street, 34th Floor  
Columbus, OH 43215

# FAQs
######  Frequently Asked Questions
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/faq-icon.svg)
Everything you need to know about The Ohio Checkbook website is at your fingertips. The collapsible sections provide users access to the most asked "help" topics.
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.
Waiting on Communications to review Text. 
* * *
The Ohio Checkbook (Checkbook.Ohio.Gov) is a first-of-its-kind government transparency website. By displaying billions of dollars in state and local government spending, Checkbook.Ohio.Gov empowers taxpayers by allowing them to see exactly how their tax dollars are spent. In November 2019, Lieutenant Governor Jon Husted and Treasurer of State Robert Sprague announced a new joint initiative to ensure Checkbook.Ohio.Gov remains a valued resource for taxpayers for years to come.
By merging the Treasurer's OhioCheckbook.com and the DeWine-Husted Administration's Interactive Budget website into one platform, The Ohio Checkbook serves as an all-in-one resource to access state and local government spending data. This streamlined effort eliminated duplication and bolstered overall reporting efficiency. 
There is no cost to local governments wishing to display spending data in The Ohio Checkbook website.
Yes. The State of Ohio Payment Card, administered through the Ohio Office of Budget and Management, is a payment tool used by state agencies to make small dollar purchases efficiently. These purchases are included in the online checkbook. 
Some expenditure data may be considered private, confidential, or protected under state or federal law. Information appearing to be private, confidential, or protected by law may not be displayed. For such expenditures, you may contact the agency for more information, but please be advised that the agency may be prohibited from releasing additional information. 
An 'Agency Journal' is either the sum of all payroll expenses for a pay period or an Agency correcting accounting chart fields that do not affect a particular supplier.
The Ohio Checkbook allows anyone to conduct �Google-like� searches of state and local spending while displaying interactive charts and graphs in a user-friendly format. Filtering and sorting features allow users to find specific information, such as keyword searches.
State expense information can be downloaded by clicking on the Spreadsheet icon located on the right side of the drop down filters and directly below the Export All header. Local and pension expense data can be downloaded by clicking the Download Visual button located at the bottom of the screen under the table information. This opens a window allowing the user to select Download CVS Spreadsheet. All data contained in The Ohio Checkbook website can be exported for full data download. A link at the bottom of each page with real-time data can be converted into multiple formats, such as: PDF, Excel (XLSX), PNG, and CVS.
If the file is opened in Excel, the 'Transaction Date' rows may not appear to be populated. Simply highlight the column, click on 'Format Cells' and select a date format. This will allow you to view all transaction dates.
The Ohio Checkbook website is compatible with Google Chrome, Safari, Edge, Firefox, Dolphin, and Opera browsers. 
No. The only individual names that may appear in The Ohio Checkbook website are state employees and individuals who have been approved as suppliers doing business with the state.
All state spending that is appropriated into a fund by the General Assembly is contained in The Ohio Checkbook website.
For questions regarding state revenue or expense data - available in The Ohio Checkbook website, please email Info@OhioCheckbook.gov. Questions concerning local expenditure data can be sent directly to local financial officers by clicking on the Questions about this Visual button at the bottom of the screen. A window will appear allowing users to fill in their contact information and submit their question. 
Yes. The Ohio Checkbook website includes gross wages, overtime, leave payments and other costs. The Ohio Checkbook website shares information from the salary database maintained by the Department of Administrative Services. According to section 125.20 of the Ohio Revised Code, the Department of Administrative Services is responsible for making state employee salary information available to the public.
There is a link at the bottom of each of the interactive pages to download a screen shot as either a PDF (PDF) document or as a PNG (PNG) image. Some visuals will allow you to download data as a spreadsheet. An icon will appear above the visual to download an Excel (XLSX) (XLSX) file of the data.
No. Ohio does not have a budget deficit. This question is usually asked by those who confuse the state budget with the federal budget. The Ohio Constitution prohibits the state from borrowing money to fund operating expenses. Therefore, the budget must be balanced.
Yes. The state credit cards are called payment cards. Payment card transactions are included in the Ohio Checkbook.
The concept of a 'surplus' is not one that is specifically defined. It is generally understood to be funds that remain above and beyond any planned uses (including planned reserves and planned carryover balances). Typically, a surplus is an unexpected result of higher-than-anticipated revenues or lower-than-anticipated spending. Amounts typically excluded from consideration as part of the surplus include one-half of one percent of GRF revenues (considered to be a necessary amount for a beginning carryover fund balance), amounts in the Budget Stabilization Fund up to 8.5% of General Revenue Fund revenues, and funds needed to support appropriations made by the General Assembly. Based on statute, state budget surpluses cannot accumulate because the law requires that any 'surplus' at the end of each fiscal year be deposited into the Income Tax Reduction Fund and returned to Ohio taxpayers.
The information displayed in this site enables anyone to see how the state is collecting, budgeting, and spending public resources. Financial information is provided in multiple formats with the capability to examine summarized data or to view the detail of individual expense transactions. Citizens can use this information to make informed decisions and provide feedback to the governor, their legislators and other public servants who work for the State of Ohio.
Press the 'control' button and '+'' (plus) button at the same time to increase the screen size of the text. Press the 'control' button and the '-'' (minus) button to decrease the size. If you wish to reset the size of text, press 'control' and '0' (zero).
The Ohio Checkbook website's data is updated daily and reflects real-time transactions completed through the prior business day.
The Ohio Checkbook data are unaudited. However, the State of Ohio's Comprehensive Annual Financial Report, which is audited, can be found on the OBM website at: https://obm.ohio.gov/wps/portal/gov/obm/areas-of-interest/state-accounting/financial-reporting/financial-reporting. 
The state's largest expenses are for Medicaid and other human services programs. This is followed by primary and secondary education and shared revenue to local governments. These payments are in the form of grants and subsidies to individuals, schools, and local governments. The Functional Categories presentation, available on the home page, best provides this information.
Managed care providers that administer Medicaid insurance programs for the state generally receive the most money from the State of Ohio. Highway construction contractors also receive significant payments for services. The Suppliers and Subsidies presentation, available on the home page, best provides this information.
Revenue and disbursement data in the Ohio Checkbook include the previous five fiscal years and the current fiscal year-to-date information. Budget data includes only the current budget year. Previous budgets can be found on the OBM website at: obm.ohio.gov/.
The Ohio Administrative Knowledge System (OAKS) is the state's accounting system which records both the spending and revenue activities of state agencies. The accounting system, maintained by the Office of Budget and Management (OBM), provides up-to-date accounting information to state government. Using OAKS, state agencies and OBM can monitor revenues and exercise control over payments and expenditures. Proper accounting of revenue and spending is necessary as part of responsible stewardship of public moneys.
The Ohio Checkbook is the singular and most trusted resource for Ohioans to obtain local and state financial information. Through a collaboration between the DeWine-Husted Administration and Ohio Treasurer's office, the new Checkbook.Ohio.Gov enhances government transparency by providing Ohioans real-time financial and transactional data.
The largest state agency in terms of dollars spent is the Department of Medicaid followed by the Department of Education. These two cabinet-level agencies provide grants and subsidies to individuals, health care providers and local schools. The Department of Taxation allocates tax revenues to local governments and pays tax refunds to individuals and businesses. The Agency Budgets and the Agency Expenses presentations, available on the home page, best provide this information.
A searchable glossary called �Glossary of Terms' is available by clicking on the �Resources' link in the footer, which is at the bottom of the website. Users are then directed to a compilation of terms and languages including definitions used within The Ohio Checkbook website.
The Office of Budget and Management (OBM) holds primary responsibility over the financial transactions of the state. As such, the director of OBM is the state's chief financial officer. Visit OBM's website at obm.ohio.gov for more information. 
The state's largest source of revenue is received from taxes, specifically income taxes and sales taxes. Other significant revenue comes from the federal government to support many programs including Medicaid and transportation. The Revenues presentation, available on the home page, best provides this information.
The state's revenue data generates from the Ohio Administrative Knowledge System (OAKS), the state's accounting system. The state accounting system enables the Office of Budget and Management (OBM) director to monitor and control both spending and revenue activities of state agencies. The accounting system, operated by OBM, provides real-time reporting of accounting information for state government.
All major web browsers are supported: Google Chrome, Mozilla Firefox, and Opera.
Any questions regarding the data contained on the Ohio Checkbook can be asked by filling out the Help/Contact Us form or emailing Questions@ohiocheckbook.gov. 
Most information related to payments made by the state is public information. If state or federal law does not protect the identity of a payee, it is included on the Ohio Checkbook website.
As the state's chief financial officer, the director of the Office of Budget and Management is responsible - pursuant to section 126.21 of the Ohio Revised Code - to maintain the accounting system of the state. As a public servant, the director desires to make this information available to the public by establishing and maintaining a searchable online database displaying real-time financial information from the state's accounting system.
Some drills terminate prior to individual transactions to protect against the release of personal and/or confidential information or the information is currently not available.
Expenses may appear to exceed the budget or appropriated amount especially near fiscal year end. This occurs when a portion of an expense is paid from an encumbrance (i.e., a reservation made in the accounting system against a prior budget year appropriation) to pay for an obligation which was incurred in that prior year.
The Ohio Checkbook website provides a high-level of transparency sharing data legally defined as public information. However, some information is considered confidential and/or personal and is protected by law. Examples include certain payments to individuals, such as social services payments (payments made to an individual for cash assistance, medical and other health-related or welfare-related benefits or services, education and training benefits or aging services) and other programs that provide direct monetary payments to an individual. Accordingly, some information is not contained in the state accounting system and will not be included on the Ohio Checkbook website.
The Ohio Checkbook website provides citizens a comprehensive view of both state and local government financial activities. It is the most trusted resource for Ohioans to access this information offered with a high-level of transparency sought by both public servants and private citizens.

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

The State of Ohio assumes no responsibility or liability for any and all non-state data or information contained on this website or use thereof.

# Counties
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/county-icon.svg)
Local government information featured on the Ohio Checkbook shows local spending grouped by Counties. Users can filter and display data down to the single transaction level.
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards. 
[ ![Ohio Checkbook Logo](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Logos/Checkbook-main-logo-2.svg) ![Ohio Checkbook Logo](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Logos/Checkbook-mobile-logo-2.svg) ](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/)

Funds](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Pensions/)
[ ![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Graphics/covid_btn.png)](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Coronavirus/)
Local government information featured on the Ohio Checkbook is provided on a voluntarily basis by counties, cities, villages, townships, school districts, libraries and other districts funded by public tax dollars. Filters allow users to view financial data by fund, department, object and/or payee. Data may be filtered and displayed in detail down to the single transaction level.
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.
[Cities & Villages ![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/cityvillage-icon.svg)](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Local/CitiesVillagesList.aspx) [Townships ![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/township-icon.svg)](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Local/TownshipsList.aspx) [Counties ![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/county-icon.svg)](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Local/CountiesList.aspx) [School Districts ![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/schools-icon.svg)](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Local/SchoolsList.aspx) [Special Districts ![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/specialdistricts-icon.svg)](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Local/SpecialDistrictsList.aspx)
**Ohio Office of Budget and Management**  
30 E. Broad Street, 34th Floor  
Columbus, OH 43215

**Ohio Treasurer**  
30 E. Broad Street, 9th Floor  
Columbus, OH 43215

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

# Townships
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/township-icon.svg)
Local government information featured on the Ohio Checkbook shows local spending grouped by Townships. Users can drill to additional levels of detail terminating at individual transactions.
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

Results: 
[State   
of Ohio](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/State/) [Local Gov   
& Schools](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Local/) [All   
Salaries](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Salaries/) [Pension   
Funds](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Pensions/)
[ ![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Graphics/covid_btn.png)](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Coronavirus/)
Ohio's pension systems are public entities structured as separate qualified independent trust funds, and therefore are not considered state agencies nor found in the state budget. The funds are governed by independent retirement boards made up of elected and appointed members, who serve as fiduciaries.
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

AN UNKNOWN ERROR HAS OCCURED
Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.

Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

# State Employee Salaries
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/state-icon.svg)
Employee salaries can be viewed by state agency or further in detail by an individual state employee. Gross wages may include, but are not limited to: on duty, leave conversion, separation leave payout, overtime and base earnings. Some employees may not have worked a complete year in their current position so gross wages may not be equivalent to full annual salary. For questions or more information, please contact Questions@OhioCheckbook.gov .
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.

# Search
Use the field below to search the Checkbook website. This search bar does not search employee salaries or pension fund recipients, please go directly to those visuals, and use the embedded search tools. Currently, the search shows results for Local Municipalities and School Districts but not their payees.

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

![](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/Gifs/large-loader-snake.gif%20) Sending Message - Please do not close this window
AN UNKNOWN ERROR HAS OCCURED
Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
**[DataOhio Portal](https://data.ohio.gov/wps/portal/gov/data/view/ohio-checkbook)** to download a comprehensive report of State data _(does not include local government and school districts data)._

# State Agency Overview 
###### Budgets and Expenses for Individual State Agencies
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/state-agency-icon.svg)
The State Agency Overview presentation allows the user to choose one state agency at a time and shows a breakdown of the state budget by expense account and the associated agency appropriation line items (ALIs). This view also shows the amount of funding that has been appropriated to each agency in the current fiscal year and what each agency has spent in the fiscal year-to-date. Information on the Agency Overview pages is not drillable. More detailed information is available in other areas on The Ohio Checkbook website.
[List All State of Ohio Agencies ](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/State/Agencies/StateAgenciesList.aspx)
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.
[List All State of Ohio Agencies ](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/State/Agencies/StateAgenciesList.aspx)
![](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/Gifs/large-loader-snake.gif%20) Loading...

AN UNKNOWN ERROR HAS OCCURED
Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

# Pension Employee Salaries
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/pension-icon.svg)
_The Ohio Public Employees Retirement System (PERS), Ohio Highway Patrol Retirement System (HPRS), Ohio Police & Fire Pension Fund (OPF), State Teachers Retirement System (STRS), and School Employees Retirement System of Ohio (SERS) all display salary data on the Ohio Checkbook. PERS and HPRS data reflects calendar years. STRS, SERS, and OPF data reflects fiscal years._
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.
![](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/Gifs/large-loader-snake.gif%20) Loading...

_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.

[ ![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Graphics/covid_btn.png)](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Coronavirus/)
All gross wage information contained in these reports come from either the Ohio Department of Administrative Services, Ohio Department of Education, Local Government Entity, or Public Pension Fund including any errors, omissions, or inaccuracies. Gross wages may include, but are not limited to, overtime, compensatory time, sick leave, vacation leave, personal leave, cost savings day deductions and leave payouts. Some employees may not have worked a complete year in their current position so gross wages may not be equivalent to full annual salary. For questions or more information, please contact Questions@OhioCheckbook.gov .

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

# State Budgets 
###### How Ohio distributes funds to State Agencies  
(Grouped by Category)
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/state-budget-icon.svg)
The State Agency Budgets presentation shows a breakdown of the State budget by functional category and the associated agency appropriation line items (ALIs). This view also shows the amount of funding that has been appropriated to each agency in the current fiscal year and what each agency has spent in the fiscal year-to-date. Drilling on an agency ALI will display its current appropriation and identify the original/enacted appropriation and any subsequent authorized actions that have adjusted that original appropriation.
* * *
Fund Total Budgeted Operating Budget Capital Budget
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.

AN UNKNOWN ERROR HAS OCCURED
Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

![](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/Gifs/large-loader-snake.gif%20) Sending Message - Please do not close this window
AN UNKNOWN ERROR HAS OCCURED
Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
**[DataOhio Portal](https://data.ohio.gov/wps/portal/gov/data/view/ohio-checkbook)** to download a comprehensive report of State data _(does not include local government and school districts data)._

AN UNKNOWN ERROR HAS OCCURED
Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

# State Budgets 
###### How Ohio distributes funds to State Agencies  
(Grouped by Category)
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/state-budget-icon.svg)
The State Agency Budgets presentation shows a breakdown of the State budget by functional category and the associated agency appropriation line items (ALIs). This view also shows the amount of funding that has been appropriated to each agency in the current fiscal year and what each agency has spent in the fiscal year-to-date. Drilling on an agency ALI will display its current appropriation and identify the original/enacted appropriation and any subsequent authorized actions that have adjusted that original appropriation.
* * *

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

# State Budgets 
###### How Ohio distributes funds to State Agencies  
(Grouped by Category)
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/state-budget-icon.svg)
The State Agency Budgets presentation shows a breakdown of the State budget by functional category and the associated agency appropriation line items (ALIs). This view also shows the amount of funding that has been appropriated to each agency in the current fiscal year and what each agency has spent in the fiscal year-to-date. Drilling on an agency ALI will display its current appropriation and identify the original/enacted appropriation and any subsequent authorized actions that have adjusted that original appropriation.
* * *
Fund Total Budgeted Operating Budget Capital Budget

**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

# State Budgets 
###### How Ohio distributes funds to State Agencies  
(Grouped by Category)
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/state-budget-icon.svg)
The State Agency Budgets presentation shows a breakdown of the State budget by functional category and the associated agency appropriation line items (ALIs). This view also shows the amount of funding that has been appropriated to each agency in the current fiscal year and what each agency has spent in the fiscal year-to-date. Drilling on an agency ALI will display its current appropriation and identify the original/enacted appropriation and any subsequent authorized actions that have adjusted that original appropriation.
* * *
Fund Total Budgeted Operating Budget Capital Budget
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.

![](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/Gifs/large-loader-snake.gif%20) Sending Message - Please do not close this window
AN UNKNOWN ERROR HAS OCCURED
Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
**[DataOhio Portal](https://data.ohio.gov/wps/portal/gov/data/view/ohio-checkbook)** to download a comprehensive report of State data _(does not include local government and school districts data)._

AN UNKNOWN ERROR HAS OCCURED
Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

# Expenses By Type  - Transportation
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/state-expenses-type.svg)
The Expense Types presentation shows spending for Ohio agencies grouped by the type of expense. Users can drill to agency and individual transactions.
* * *
Fund Total Budgeted Operating Budget Capital Budget
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.
![](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/Gifs/large-loader-snake.gif%20) Loading...

Marks Selection: 
URL Parameters: 
Download Visual  Get Short URL  Questions about this Visual 
![](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/Gifs/large-loader-snake.gif%20) Sending Message - Please do not close this window
AN UNKNOWN ERROR HAS OCCURED
Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
**[DataOhio Portal](https://data.ohio.gov/wps/portal/gov/data/view/ohio-checkbook)** to download a comprehensive report of State data _(does not include local government and school districts data)._
**Short URL to Share Page:**
A Short URL could not be created, use the following URL to share this page with others:
_https://checkbook.ohio.gov/State/Expenses/Type.aspx?agency=Department+of+Transportation%2CPublic+Works+Commission &appropriation+type=Total&level=EC1-ExpCat&pagetitle=Transportation_

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

# State Spending by County
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/county-icon.svg)
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.
Performance Test: 
Marks Selection: 
URL Parameters: 
Download Visual  Get Short URL  Questions about this Visual 
![](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/Gifs/large-loader-snake.gif%20) Sending Message - Please do not close this window
AN UNKNOWN ERROR HAS OCCURED
Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
**[DataOhio Portal](https://data.ohio.gov/wps/portal/gov/data/view/ohio-checkbook)** to download a comprehensive report of State data _(does not include local government and school districts data)._

# Expenses By Functional Category  - Justice+and+Public+Protection
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/state-expenses-category.svg)
The Functional Category presentation shows state agency spending grouped into nine broad categories based on the function or type of service provided to the citizens of Ohio. Users can drill through increasing levels of detail all the way to individual transactions.
* * *
Fund Total Budgeted Operating Budget Capital Budget
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.

# Expenses By Functional Category 
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/state-expenses-category.svg)
The Functional Category presentation shows state agency spending grouped into nine broad categories based on the function or type of service provided to the citizens of Ohio. Users can drill through increasing levels of detail all the way to individual transactions.
* * *
Fund Total Budgeted Operating Budget Capital Budget
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.

AN UNKNOWN ERROR HAS OCCURED
Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.

![](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/Gifs/large-loader-snake.gif%20) Sending Message - Please do not close this window
AN UNKNOWN ERROR HAS OCCURED
Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.

# State General Revenue Fund
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/state-popular/grf-icon.svg)
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.
# State General Revenue Fund
###### Year End Balance
The General Revenue Fund (GRF) balance presentation shows the historical and estimated balances of the GRF through the current fiscal year on a cash basis and on a "fund" basis. The unencumbered and unobligated "fund" balance is calculated by deducting the amount reserved for prior year encumbrances and the amount reserved for obligations authorized by the General Assembly (i.e., designated transfers) from that fiscal year's ending cash balance.
![](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/Gifs/large-loader-snake.gif%20) Loading...

Ending Cash Balance1 | 4,721,519 | ![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Other/table-arrow-bottom.png) | 6,547,038 | ![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Other/table-arrow-bottom.png) | 8,990,659 | ![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Other/table-arrow-bottom.png) | 2,141,622 | ![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Other/table-arrow-bottom.png) | 2,012,628  
Reservations for Prior Year Encumbrances | 689,255 |  | 883,540 |  | 1,633,516 |  | 1,050,466 |  | -  
Unencumbered Ending Cash Balance | 4,032,265 |  | 5,663,498 |  | 7,357,143 |  | 1,091,156 |  | 2,012,628  
0.5% Balance Requirement  | 197,731 |  | 203,301 |  | 212,576 |  | 206,665 |  | 220,976  
Surplus Ending Balance & Disposition2 | 3,834,533 |  | 5,460,197 |  | 7,144,566 |  | 884,491 |  | 1,791,652  
Reservations for Designated Transfers3 |  1,498,300  |  | - |  | 4,672,954 |  | - |  | -  
Transfer to the Budget Stabilization Fund | - |  | - |  | - |  | - |  | -  
Transfer to the Income Tax Reduction Fund | - |  | - |  | - |  | - |  | -  
Authorized Retained Balance4 | 2,336,233 |  | 5,460,197 |  | 2,471,612 |  | 884,491 |  | 1,791,652  
1 Cash balance equals the amount of moneys available on a cash (non-accrual) basis to support appropriations, including authorized transfers and encumbrances. The beginning cash balance includes reservations for both prior year encumbrances and designated transfers from the prior year ending balance. 
2 Surplus ending balance equals the ending cash balance less prior year encumbrances and less the 0.5% ending balance requirement of ORC Section 131.44.
3 Designated transfers are established in Acts passed by the General Assembly and include transfers to the unemployment compensation interest fund, medicaid reserve fund, disaster relief and emergency purposes funds, and other funds for one-time uses. 
4 The authorized retained balance reflects monies set aside pursuant to law for specific purposes such as pre-funding the cost of the subsequent fiscal years income tax reductions. More information regarding disposition of the GRF surplus ending balance in a particular fiscal year is available on the OBM website in the July edition of that year's Monthly Financial Report.

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

AN UNKNOWN ERROR HAS OCCURED
Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.

# Revenue Flow of Funds
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/state-revenues-flow.svg)
The State Revenue Flow of Funds presentation shows the source and amount of revenue deposited into a particular state fund (or budget fund group) and expenditures from the fund by purpose or expense account. The amount of revenue deposited into and the amount of expenditures from a fund over a specified time period may not be equal due to changes in the cash balance over that same time period.
* * *
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.

![](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/Gifs/large-loader-snake.gif%20) Sending Message - Please do not close this window
AN UNKNOWN ERROR HAS OCCURED
Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
**[DataOhio Portal](https://data.ohio.gov/wps/portal/gov/data/view/ohio-checkbook)** to download a comprehensive report of State data _(does not include local government and school districts data)._

# Revenue in Detail
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/state-revenues-detail.svg)
The State Revenue Detail presentation shows users state revenues by increasing level of detail starting with account and progressing to agency and fund levels.

AN UNKNOWN ERROR HAS OCCURED
Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.

# Suppliers, Subsidies and Refunds, Other Payments
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/state-popular/companies-icon.svg)
The Supplier, Subsidy and Other presentation depicts payments to suppliers, subsidy payments, and other payments consisting primarily of state expenses including payroll and debt service payments. Users can drill through increasing levels of detail all the way to individual transactions. Note that small percentage amounts of payments may not appear on the graph. Select the click the "click to view all transactions for...." link to view a list of the transaction details.
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.
Performance Test: 
Marks Selection: 
URL Parameters: 
Download Visual  Get Short URL  Questions about this Visual 
![](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/Gifs/large-loader-snake.gif%20) Sending Message - Please do not close this window
AN UNKNOWN ERROR HAS OCCURED
Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.

Any questions and/or information submitted to the State of Ohio may constitute a public record and thus may be released in response to a public records request. By submitting this message you acknowledge and accept these terms. Form more information please see our [Privacy Policy.](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/About/PrivacyPolicy.aspx)
## Top Subsidies and Refund Descriptions
**ACH-Public Employees Retirement System**
> Payments made to the Public Employees Retirement System for employer and employee share of retirement plan.
**Aetna Better Health Inc**
> One of several Medicaid managed care providers selected by the Department of Medicaid to provide Medicaid health benefits and related services to enrolled Ohioans. The Department of Medicaid typically pays a fixed, per capita fee to the providers for enrollees.
**Buckeye Community Health Plan**
> One of several Medicaid managed care providers selected by the Department of Medicaid to provide Medicaid health benefits and related services to enrolled Ohioans. The Department of Medicaid typically pays a fixed, per capita fee to the providers for enrollees.
**Caresource**
> One of several Medicaid managed care providers selected by the Department of Medicaid to provide Medicaid health benefits and related services to enrolled Ohioans. The Department of Medicaid typically pays a fixed, per capita fee to the providers for enrollees.
**Catamaran RX**
> One of several healthcare insurance providers to state employees.
**Coding Changes**
> Accounting entries that are made to adjust or correct the coding of expenses. These entries are done by general journal rather than by individual transaction and exclude changes to transactions that include confidential and personal information. 
**Commissioners of the Sinking Fund**
> The Commissioners of the Sinking Fund, administered by the Treasurer of State receives payments of bond principle and interest from state agency debt service appropriations then in turn pays the holders of the bonds.
**Debt Service**
> The payment of principal, interest, and associated costs on the state's bonded indebtedness. Debt service appropriations are usually made to the agency on whose behalf the bonds were issued.
**Department of Administrative Services**
> This state agency provides centralized services such as IT, procurement, human resources and printing to other state agencies. Costs of those services are recovered by direct and indirect charges to the agencies for the services provided.
**Department of Developmental Disabilities**
> This state agency provides services that are partially funded by Federal Medicaid grants administered by the Ohio Department of Medicaid and other state agencies. Services include Medicaid waivers, intermediate care facilities and state run developmental care facilities.
**Lottery Prizes**
> Payments made by the Lottery Commission to lottery winners and selling vendors. The Ohio Lottery Commission maintains a record of recipient payments.
**Medical Mutual of Ohio**
> One of several healthcare insurance providers to state employees.
**Molina Healthcare of Ohio**
> One of several Medicaid managed care providers selected by the Department of Medicaid to provide Medicaid health benefits and related services to enrolled Ohioans. The Department of Medicaid typically pays a fixed, per capita fee to the providers for enrollees.
**Paramount Advantage**
> One of several Medicaid managed care providers selected by the Department of Medicaid to provide Medicaid health benefits and related services to enrolled Ohioans. The Department of Medicaid typically pays a fixed, per capita fee to the providers for enrollees.
**Public Assistance Recipient**
> Individuals that receive public assistance from federal and state programs such as Temporary Aid to Needy Children, foster care, adoption assistance and medically handicapped child services. While transactions are reported, individual names are withheld.
**School Employees Retirement System**
> The Department of Education withholds state funding to local school districts and pays these school districts' share of retirement plan payments into the School Employees Retirement System.
**State Payroll Expense**
> Wages and salaries paid by the state to its employees. These costs include fringe benefits and related administrative charges.
**State Teachers Retirement System**
> The Department of Education withholds state funding to local school districts and pays these school districts' share of retirement plan payments into the State Teachers Retirement System.
**Tax and Settlement Distributions**
> Payments made pursuant to adjudicated determinations and decisions often involving disputed tax payments.
**The Ohio State University**
> State colleges and universities receive capital project appropriations from the State of Ohio. Monies are paid from the State's accounting systems to the individual school's accounting system - in this case the Ohio State University. Ohio state also provides services to state agencies and receives payments from those agencies.
**Treasurer of State**
> The Treasurer of State receives payments of bond principle and interest from state agency debt service appropriations then in turn pays the holders of the bonds. The Treasurer of State also makes payments to the Federal government on behalf of agencies and provides banking services to state agencies.
**United Health Group**
> One of several Medicaid managed care providers selected by the Department of Medicaid to provide Medicaid health benefits and related services to enrolled Ohioans. The Department of Medicaid typically pays a fixed, per capita fee to the providers for enrollees.
**United Healthcare Community Plan of Ohio**
> One of several Medicaid managed care providers selected by the Department of Medicaid to provide Medicaid health benefits and related services to enrolled Ohioans. The Department of Medicaid typically pays a fixed, per capita fee to the providers for enrollees.
**Ohio Office of Budget and Management**  
30 E. Broad Street, 34th Floor  
Columbus, OH 43215

[Questions@OhioCheckbook.gov](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Contact/)
**Ohio Treasurer**  
30 E. Broad Street, 9th Floor  
Columbus, OH 43215

# ALI Expense Breakdown  - Medicaid
![](https://checkbook.ohio.gov/Images/Icons/state-icon.svg)
Putting government **transparency** at your fingertips.
### Please select a fund:
- Select One -  Appropriation Line Item Group Load Visual
Performance Test: 
Marks Selection: 
URL Parameters: 
Download Visual  Get Short URL  Questions about this Visual 
![](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/Gifs/large-loader-snake.gif%20) Sending Message - Please do not close this window
AN UNKNOWN ERROR HAS OCCURED
Select a file type to download:
Download PDF  Download Image  Download CSV Spreadsheet  View Data 
_"Unexpected Server Error"_ when trying to **View Data** or **Download CSV** , please select a data element in the chart first, then try downloading again. If the error message persists with the CSV option, you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
_blank CSV file_ , please select a data element in the chart or click in any white space, then try downloading again. If the file is still blank you can also download a CSV within the **View Data** screen by selecting the "Download all rows as a text file" button.
**[DataOhio Portal](https://data.ohio.gov/wps/portal/gov/data/view/ohio-checkbook)** to download a comprehensive report of State data _(does not include local government and school districts data)._

An official State of Ohio site.  Here's how you know 
![Ohio .Gov Logo](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohio-stateLogo.svg)
**Official websites use _Ohio.gov_** An Ohio.gov website belongs to an official government organization in the State of Ohio. 
**Secure _.gov_ websites use HTTPS** A lock _https://_ means you've safely connected to the .gov website. Share sensitive information only on official, secure websites. 
**Trusted applications are secured by![OHID](https://webresources.obm.ohio.gov/SharedFiles/Images/logos/ohid_logo.png) ** When you log in with OHID, your privacy, data, and personal information are protected by federal and state digital security standards.
